<script>

    function getAppTypeCookie(){
        var cookies = document.cookie.split(';').reduce((acc, string) => {
            const [key, value] = string.split('=');
            return {...acc, [key.trim()]: value}
        }, {})

        var appTypeCookie = cookies['app-type']

        if(appTypeCookie){
            return appTypeCookie
        }

        return '';
    }

    function repositionComponents(){
        var logoWrapper = document.querySelector('.logo-wrapper');
        var backIconWrapper = document.querySelector('.back-icon-wrapper');
        var logo = document.querySelector('.logo');
        var svgLogoWrapper = document.querySelector('.logo-wrapper .svg-logo-wrapper')
        var userWrapper = document.querySelector('.user-wrapper');
        var userDropdownMenu = document.querySelector('.user-wrapper .dropdown-menu')
        var isCheckout = document.location.pathname.includes('checkout');
        var isBackVisible = backIconWrapper && backIconWrapper.style.display !== 'none';

        logoWrapper.style.order = -1;
        logo.style.width = 'fit-content';
        if(isCheckout){
            logo.style.paddingLeft = '24px';
        }
        if(isCheckout && !isBackVisible){
            logo.style.transform = 'none';
        }
        logo.style.alignItems = 'center';
        svgLogoWrapper.style.transform = "scale(0.8) translateX(-15%)";
        userWrapper.style.order = 5;

        if(userDropdownMenu){
            userDropdownMenu.style.left = '-140px';
        }

        if(!document.referrer.includes('foodpanda')){
            logo.style.paddingLeft = '24px';
        }
    }

    var appTypeCookie = getAppTypeCookie();
    if(appTypeCookie === 'gcashmweb' && window.innerWidth < 960){
        repositionComponents()
    }

</script>

			<h2 class="h4"><strong>Our goal is to make food delivery fast, easy and convenient!</strong></h2>
			<p align="justify">
				If you're looking for a <b>food delivery service</b> in Singapore that offers fast convenience whenever you want it, you’re just at the right spot. Founded in 2012, we've made it our goal to simplify your life by making food delivery as convenient and affordable as possible whilst taking you with us on a culinary journey around the world. We've even added online grocery shopping and more to our app, letting you order everything from fresh to frozen food and more from shops like Marks &amp; Spencer and 7-Eleven. Among dozens of eateries, family businesses and high-class restaurants, one is often hard pressed to make a choice for lunch, breakfast or dinner; with the foodpanda mobile app or website, you can access the menus of over 500 restaurants in Singapore and order your favourite meal online in just a few clicks!</p>

<h3><strong>Frequently Asked Questions</strong></h3>
  <div itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
    <h4 itemprop="name"><strong>How can I get foodpanda delivery?</strong></h4>
    <div itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
      <div itemprop="text">
      <p>To get foodpanda delivery, just find a restaurant or shop you want to order from by entering your postcode, look through the menu and choose your items. When you are happy with your selection, click on the "ORDER NOW" button, confirm your delivery adress and make a payment. You will receive an email and SMS confirming the order and delivery time.</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

<div itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
    <h4 itemprop="name"><strong>How can I order food in Singapore?</strong></h4>
    <div itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
      <div itemprop="text">
      <p>This is how to order food on foodpanda in Singapore:
</p><ol>
<li><strong> Find a restaurant.</strong> Enter your address on the home page. Browse our extensive list of restaurants and shops that deliver to your area. Pick one of our partners and look through the menu.</li>
<li> <strong>Choose your dishes.</strong> Browse the menu and select dishes you would like to order. Your items will appear on your cart on the right.</li>
<li> <strong>Checkout &amp; Payment.</strong> Once you are happy with your order, click on the "ORDER NOW" button and enter your delivery address. Simply follow the checkout instructions from there.</li>
<li> <strong>Delivery. </strong>We will send you an email and SMS confirming your order and delivery time. Sit back, relax and wait for piping hot food to be conveniently delivered to you! </li>
</ol>
<p></p>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

	<div itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
  <h4 itemprop="name"><strong>What is the difference between delivery and Pick-Up?</strong></h4>
  <div itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
    <div itemprop="text">
      <p>If you choose delivery, a foodpanda rider will collect your order from the restaurant and take it to your chosen delivery address. If you choose Pick-Up, you can self-collect your food directly from the restaurant for extra savings – and to jump to the front of the queue. Pick-Up orders are available for restaurants only. </p>

var acc = document.getElementsByClassName("accordion");
var i;

for (i = 0; i < acc.length; i++) {
  acc[i].onclick = function() {
    this.classList.toggle("active");
    var panel = this.nextElementSibling;
    if (panel.style.maxHeight){
      panel.style.maxHeight = null;
    } else {
      panel.style.maxHeight = panel.scrollHeight + "px";
    } 
  }
}
